// begin file /f/release1/usr/include/PR/abi.h


typedef struct {
    /* 0x0 */ unsigned int cmd : 8;
    /* 0x1 */ unsigned int flags : 8;
    /* 0x2 */ unsigned int gain : 16;
    /* 0x4 */ unsigned int addr;
} Aadpcm;


typedef struct {
    /* 0x0 */ unsigned int cmd : 8;
    /* 0x1 */ unsigned int flags : 8;

typedef union {
